        </div></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <p>Andorra is famous for the practice of <a href="/wiki/Winter_sports" title="Winter sports">winter sports</a>. Andorra has the largest territory of ski slopes in the <a href="/wiki/Pyrenees" title="Pyrenees">Pyrenees</a> (3100 hectares and about 350&nbsp;km of slopes) and two ski resorts. Grandvalira is the largest and most popular resort. Other popular sports played in Andorra include <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a>, <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Roller_hockey_(quad)" title="Roller hockey (quad)">roller hockey</a>. </p>
      <p>For <a href="/wiki/Roller_hockey_(quad)" title="Roller hockey (quad)">roller hockey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_roller_hockey_team" title="Andorra national roller hockey team">Andorra</a> usually plays in <a href="/wiki/CERH_European_Roller_Hockey_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="CERH European Roller Hockey Championship">CERH Euro Cup</a> and in <a href="/wiki/FIRS_Roller_Hockey_World_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="FIRS Roller Hockey World Cup">FIRS Roller Hockey World Cup</a>. In 2011, Andorra was the host country to the <a href="/wiki/2011_European_League_Final_Eight" class="mw-redirect" title="2011 European League Final Eight">2011 European League Final Eight</a>. </p>
      <p>The country is represented in association football by the <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra national football team</a>. The team gained its first competitive win in a European Championship qualifier on 11 October 2019, against Moldova.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">[215]</a></sup> Football is governed in Andorra by the <a href="/wiki/Andorran_Football_Federation" title="Andorran Football Federation">Andorran Football Federation</a> - founded in 1994, it organizes the national competitions of association football (<a href="/wiki/Primera_Divisi%C3%B3" title="Primera Divisió">Primera Divisió</a>, <a href="/wiki/Copa_Constituci%C3%B3" title="Copa Constitució">Copa Constitució</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andorran_Supercup" title="Andorran Supercup">Supercopa</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Futsal" title="Futsal">futsal</a>. Andorra was admitted to <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> and <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> in the same year, 1996. <a href="/wiki/FC_Andorra" title="FC Andorra">FC Andorra</a>, a club based in <a href="/wiki/Andorra_la_Vella" title="Andorra la Vella">Andorra la Vella</a> founded in 1942, compete in the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_football_league_system" title="Spanish football league system">Spanish football league system</a>. </p>
      <p><a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">Rugby</a> is a traditional sport in Andorra, mainly influenced by the popularity in southern France. The <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_rugby_union_team" title="Andorra national rugby union team">Andorra national rugby union team</a>, nicknamed Els Isards, plays on the international stage in <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rugby_sevens" title="Rugby sevens">rugby sevens</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">[216]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/VPC_Andorra_XV" title="VPC Andorra XV">VPC Andorra XV</a> is a rugby team based in Andorra la Vella actually playing in the French championship. </p>
      <p>Basketball popularity has increased in the country since the 1990s, when the Andorran team <a href="/wiki/BC_Andorra" title="BC Andorra">BC Andorra</a> played in the top league of Spain (<a href="/wiki/Liga_ACB" title="Liga ACB">Liga ACB</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">[217]</a></sup> After 18 years the club returned to the top league in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">[218]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Other sports practised in Andorra include cycling, volleyball, judo, Australian Rules football, handball, swimming, gymnastics, tennis, and motorsports. In 2012, Andorra raised its first national cricket team and played a home match against the Dutch Fellowship of Fairly Odd Places Cricket Club, the first match played in the history of Andorra at an altitude of 1,300 metres (4,300&nbsp;ft).<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">[219]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Andorra first participated at the <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Games" title="Olympic Games">Olympic Games</a> in 1976. The country has appeared in every <a href="/wiki/Winter_Olympic" class="mw-redirect" title="Winter Olympic">Winter Olympic</a> Games since <a href="/wiki/1976_Winter_Olympics" title="1976 Winter Olympics">1976</a>. Andorra competes in the <a href="/wiki/Games_of_the_Small_States_of_Europe" title="Games of the Small States of Europe">Games of the Small States of Europe</a>, being twice the host country in <a href="/wiki/1991_Games_of_the_Small_States_of_Europe" title="1991 Games of the Small States of Europe">1991</a> and <a href="/wiki/2005_Games_of_the_Small_States_of_Europe" title="2005 Games of the Small States of Europe">2005</a>. </p>
      <p>As one of the <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Countries" title="Catalan Countries">Catalan Countries</a>, Andorra is home to a team of <a href="/wiki/Castell" title="Castell">castellers</a>, or Catalan human tower builders. The <a href="/w/index.php?title=Castellers_d%27Andorra&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Castellers d'Andorra (page does not exist)">Castellers d'Andorra</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://ca.wikipedia.org/wiki/Castellers_d%27Andorra" class="extiw" title="ca:Castellers d'Andorra">ca</a>]</span>, based in the town of <a href="/wiki/Santa_Coloma_d%27Andorra" title="Santa Coloma d'Andorra">Santa Coloma d'Andorra</a>, are recognized by the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Coordinadora_de_Colles_Castelleres_de_Catalunya&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Coordinadora de Colles Castelleres de Catalunya (page does not exist)">Coordinadora de Colles Castelleres de Catalunya</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://ca.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coordinadora_de_Colles_Castelleres_de_Catalunya" class="extiw" title="ca:Coordinadora de Colles Castelleres de Catalunya">ca</a>]</span>, the governing body of castells. </p>

                 <div>
                  <div class="plainlist">
                   <ul>
                    <li><sup>1</sup> <a href="/wiki/Island#Oceanic_islands" title="Island">Oceanic islands</a> within the vicinity of Europe are usually grouped with the continent even though they are not situated on its continental shelf.</li>
                    <li><sup>2</sup> Some countries completely outside the conventional geographical boundaries of Europe are commonly associated with the continent due to ethnological links.</li>
                   </ul>
